## Sdk        in package    - [Aws](package-aws.md)

#### createClient()  [header link](class-aws-sdk-method-createclient.md)

Get a client by name using an array of constructor options.

`
    public
                    createClient(string $name[, array<string|int, mixed> $args = [] ]) : AwsClientInterface`

##### Parameters

$name
: string

Service name or namespace (e.g., DynamoDb, s3).

$args
: array<string\|int, mixed>
= \[\]

Arguments to configure the client.

##### Tags  [header link](class-aws-sdk-method-createclient-tags.md)

throwsInvalidArgumentException

if any required options are missing or
the service is not supported.

seeAwsClient::\_\_construct

for a list of available options for args.

##### Return values

[AwsClientInterface](class-aws-awsclientinterface.md)
